          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Sunday, January 19, 2014</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://www.chinaforeignteachersunion.org/2014/01/china-foreign-teachers-union-china.html'>China Foreign Teachers Union: China Foreign Teacher Salaries/Pay Almost Lowest In The World</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-8157056434890850227' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
<div style="text-align: justify;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><i><b><span style="color: #20124d;">Looking For The 2018 CFTU Blacklist?</span></b></i>&nbsp; Click Here: </span><br />

<br />

<span style="color: #20124d;"><a href="http://reddit.com/r/chinascamcentral">http://reddit.com/r/chinascamcentral</a></span><br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-ufbVZ_QbAd4/UtxhXmuVLzI/AAAAAAAAAms/qsfVwt-dvgw/s1600/chinese_yuan_symbol_m.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-ufbVZ_QbAd4/UtxhXmuVLzI/AAAAAAAAAms/qsfVwt-dvgw/s1600/chinese_yuan_symbol_m.jpg" width="222" /></a></div>
<div align="center">
&#65279;</div>
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">The Huffington Post has just recently confirmed what we have been complaining about for 2 years - the pay of foreign teachers in China is 40% less than the world average and is not keeping pace with other professions in China. Now only 17 countries pay teachers lower wages in the world than China&nbsp; <i>(Scroll down for charts)</i></span></div>
<br />
<div style="text-align: center;">
<a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2013/10/03/average-teacher-salary-around-world_n_4037534.html"><span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: x-large;">Huffington Post Report</span></a></div>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-tBFaXlDPXNM/Utxc1vqI3CI/AAAAAAAAAmg/O5YLpo6BbZo/s1600/teacher-salary-by-country.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="371" src="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-tBFaXlDPXNM/Utxc1vqI3CI/AAAAAAAAAmg/O5YLpo6BbZo/s1600/teacher-salary-by-country.png" width="640" /></a></div>
<div align="center">
&#65279;</div>
<br />
<div style="text-align: center;">
<span style="color: red;"><span lang="EN-US"><b><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: medium;">&nbsp;</span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><b><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: medium;">CHINA</span></b></span></span></div>
<div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: center;">
</div>
<div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
<span style="color: blue;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;">The </span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://www.statista.com/statistics/19323/total-population-of-china/"><span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; text-decoration: none;">total population of China</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"> has reached 1.45 million. Of this, the </span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://www.statista.com/statistics/252848/economically-active-population-vs-number-of-employed-persons-in-china/"><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; text-decoration: none;"><span style="color: #20124d;">economically active</span> <span style="color: #20124d;">population</span></span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"> was 785.79 million at the end of 2011. At that time, </span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://www.statista.com/statistics/251380/number-of-employed-persons-in-china/"><span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; text-decoration: none;">China&#8217;s workforce</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"> hit 764.2 million people, with 359.14 million employed in urban and 405 million in rural China. The </span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://www.statista.com/statistics/234578/number-of-migrant-workers-in-china/"><span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; text-decoration: none;">number of migrant workers</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"> stood at 252.78 million, with an increase of 10.55 million from 2010. Among the migrant laborers, about 158.63 million worked outside of their home province. Regarding the </span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://www.statista.com/statistics/167160/employment-by-economic-sectors-in-china/"><span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; text-decoration: none;">sectors</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;">, primary industry accounted for 34.8 percent of total employment, while secondary industry represented 29.5 percent, and tertiary industry had a share of 35.7 percent. The </span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://www.statista.com/statistics/167111/unemployment-rate-in-china/"><span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; text-decoration: none;">unemployment rate</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"> in urban China stood at 4.1 percent, and the </span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://www.statista.com/statistics/219730/number-of-unemployed-people-in-china/"><span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; text-decoration: none;">number of unemployed persons</span></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"> reached 9.2 million. Employment forecasts by the Ministry of Labor project annual growth to average 3.2% per annum over through 2015. Approximately 1.6 million foreigners are employed in China. Of those, foreigners teachers account for 82% with average salaries of 16,500 yuan per month. Average salaries for professional foreigners is 52,000 yuan per month. Currently, expat foreign teachers are the lowest paid foreigners in China.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>
<div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
<span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"><br /><span style="color: blue;"></span></span></div>
<div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
<span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;">The above information was obtained from China's Ministry of Labor. The below chart was compiled by independent CFTU research conducted by our volunteer staff over the last six months based on random surveys of 500 ESL teachers working abroad in the countries researched. This may explain why fewer teachers are coming to C</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color: white; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="color: blue;">hina</span>.</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color: red; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"> CFTU members can obtain a copy of the complete report by sending an email to admin@ChinaForeignTeachersUnion.org.</span></div>
<div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: center;">
<span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"><br /></span></div>
<div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: center;">
<span lang="EN-US" style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;">2013 &nbsp;ESL Teacher Survey</span></div>
<div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
<span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"><br /></span></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-BY9r_RfT2U0/UrlWI4ToEoI/AAAAAAAAAjo/yUmRBYAUJJU/s1600/_0_page_img_1.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="126" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-BY9r_RfT2U0/UrlWI4ToEoI/AAAAAAAAAjo/yUmRBYAUJJU/s1600/_0_page_img_1.jpg" width="400" /></a></div>
<div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
<br />
<span lang="EN-US" style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">The numbers above in the left column equate only to average monthly salaries in thousands of USD. The good news is that Chinese society still respects teachers as much as doctors and airline pilots. If only we could pay our mortgages and car payments with prestige!</span></div>
<div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
<br /></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://www.edudemic.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/teacher-status-findings-620x397.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="204" src="http://www.edudemic.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/09/teacher-status-findings-620x397.png" width="320" /></a></div>
<div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;">
<br /></div>
<div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: justify;">
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;">Below is the average pay of primary school teachers by country as compiled by UBS HR's Department. The first figure represents Annual Gross Income. The second figure represents after-tax income, and the last number represents the hours worked per week.</span></div>
<div class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: center;">

</td><td style="background-color: transparent; border-image: none; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 3.75pt;"><div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>

<span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="color: #20124d;">Managing Director / 20+ Years</span></span></div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
</td><td style="background-color: transparent; border-image: none; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 3.75pt;"><div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
<div style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;">
<span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="color: #20124d;">315K+</span></span></div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
</td><td style="background-color: transparent; border-image: none; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 3.75pt;"><div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
<div style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;">
<span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="color: #20124d;">2M+</span></span></div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
</td></tr>
<tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 20;"><td style="background-color: transparent; border-image: none; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 3.75pt;"><div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
<div style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;">
<span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="color: #20124d;">Sales/Marketing</span></span></div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
</td><td style="background-color: transparent; border-image: none; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 3.75pt;"><div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
<div style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;">
<span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="color: #20124d;">Mid-Level Manager / 7+ Years</span></span></div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
</td><td style="background-color: transparent; border-image: none; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 3.75pt;"><div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
<div style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;">
<span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="color: #20124d;">48 to 110K</span></span></div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
</td><td style="background-color: transparent; border-image: none; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 3.75pt;"><div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
<div style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;">
<span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="color: #20124d;">300 to 700K</span></span></div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
</td></tr>
<tr style="mso-yfti-irow: 21; mso-yfti-lastrow: yes;"><td style="background-color: transparent; border-image: none; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 3.75pt;"><div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
<div style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;">
<span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="color: #20124d;">Sales/Marketing</span></span></div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
</td><td style="background-color: transparent; border-image: none; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 3.75pt;"><div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
<div style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;">
<span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="color: #20124d;">Front Office Manager / 5+ Years</span></span></div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
</td><td style="background-color: transparent; border-image: none; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 3.75pt;"><div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
<div style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;">
<span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="color: #20124d;">36K</span></span></div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
</td><td style="background-color: transparent; border-image: none; border: rgb(0, 0, 0); padding: 3.75pt;"><div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></div>
<div style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;">
<span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt;"><span style="color: #20124d;">230K</span></span></div>
<span style="font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<span style="color: red; font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></span></div>
<span style="color: red; font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"> </span>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<span style="color: red; font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"> </span></span></div>
<span style="color: red; font-family: &quot;arial&quot;;"> </span>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<br /></div>
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"></span><br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: justify;">
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><span style="color: black; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;;"><span style="color: #20124d; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">*Note further that these are aggregated amounts of an average expat salary in the private sector in China: if you work for a small firm or company, expect to earn a little less; if you work for a large firm or company (or better yet, a foreign company), expect to earn a little more. The amounts quoted also assume a fair amount of relevant work experience &#8211; as a foreign worker in China, a minimum of 8 years is preferred.</span></span></span></div>
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"> </span>
<br />
<h3>
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"> <span style="color: red;">Saving potential for expats in China...</span></span></h3>
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"> </span>
<br />
<div style="text-align: justify;">
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">For many expats, the question of whether or not to emigrate to China will depend on their saving potential &#8211; i.e. how much money they can 'bank' at the end of every month, after paying tax and &nbsp;covering accommodation and living expenses.&nbsp;</span></div>
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"> </span>
<br />
<div style="text-align: justify;">
</div>
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"> </span>
<br />
<div style="text-align: justify;">
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">For highly qualified and skilled expats, this is not so much of a concern, with about 25 percent of expats in China earning in the region of USD 200K a year. For those seeking mid-level employment in China, however, the following factors should be taken into consideration:&nbsp;</span></div>
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"> </span>
<br />
<div style="text-align: justify;">
</div>
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"> </span>
<br />
<ul><span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">
<li><div style="text-align: justify;">
Although China's cost of living is famously low &#8211; with youthful ESL teachers known to live on about RMB 3,500 (USD 500) per month &#8211; your expat salary package remains very important. Try to negotiate the best possible deal for yourself, as often the 'perks' of your contract will decide whether a move to China is financially viable for you or not.</div>
</li>
</span></ul>
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"> </span>
<br />
<ul><span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">
<li><div style="text-align: justify;">
Although many Chinese employers won't provide an accommodation stipend, some will. You're doing well if they offer you something in the region of RMB 9,000 (USD 1,500) per month.</div>
</li>
</span></ul>
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"> </span>
<br />
<ul><span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">
<li><div style="text-align: justify;">
Health insurance for foreign workers in China is quite expensive, and if this is provided in your salary package, it will save you at least RMB 1,300 (USD 200) per month.</div>
</li>
</span></ul>
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"> </span><br />
<ul><span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">
<li><div style="text-align: justify;">
The issue of whether or not the company will provide for education expenses is often the 'deal-breaker' for expat families planning a move to China. The price of good-quality international education is astronomical &#8211; as much as RMB 1.2M (USD 200K) per year in the most extreme cases.</div>
</li>
</span></ul>
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"> </span><br />
<ul><span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">
<li><div style="text-align: justify;">
Bear in mind, too, that most expats will be taxed around 20% of their monthly salary in China, but that this can rise to 40% for high earners.</div>
</li>
</span></ul>
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"> </span><br />
<ul><span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">
<li><div style="text-align: justify;">
Note that as a foreign worker in China, you will be expected to work very hard for your money, and that the intensity of the Chinese workplace can be a bit overwhelming for some expats.</div>
</li>
</span></ul>
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"> </span>
<br />
<ul><span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">
<li><div style="text-align: justify;">
Remember that although working in China might not be as financially rewarding as working in other expat destinations, such as the Middle East or Russia, there are some wonderful cultural benefits to such an adventure. China is at the forefront of global economic development, and there are many exciting things happening within the country to attract ambitious professionals. Also, the opportunity to learn a bit of Mandarin is widely reported by expats to be one of the most valuable aspects of working in China.</div>
</li>
</span></ul>
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"> </span>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<br /></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Now if you need to calculate your salary,taxes,or pension in China&nbsp;</span></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<span style="color: blue; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">please use this complimentary calculator: </span><span style="color: red;"><a href="http://salary.directhr.net/">http://salary.directhr.net/</a></span><br />
<br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both;">

<div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
<span style="color: #20124d;"><b>HONEST &amp; ETHICAL CHINA EXPAT EMPLOYERS</b></span></div>
